    <h6>News - Apr 01, 2020
      (about 1 year ago)
      <span id="news-showtext" class="showtext">Click to show.</span>
    </h6>
    <div class="newsbody styled-dtext"><p>We now have a Discord server, <a rel="nofollow" class="dtext-link" href="/static/discord">come talk to us</a>!</p><ul><li><strong>April 1st:</strong> We're currently experiencing connectivity issues to some parts of the world, this does not appear to be an issue on our end we'd be able to fix, but appears to be something with Cloudflare's nodes. If you can try restarting your router / device and see if you'll be routed to a node that works as it should. Alternatively if you're using a VPN setting it to the US might help as well.</li></ul><p>Want to advertise on e621? <a rel="nofollow" class="dtext-link" href="/forum/show/10410">Click here!</a></p></div>
